\DoxyCodeLine{385         \textcolor{comment}{// 3D vector: 11/11/10 floating-\/point components}}
\DoxyCodeLine{386         \textcolor{comment}{// The 3D vector is packed into 32 bits as follows: a 5-\/bit biased exponent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{387         \textcolor{comment}{// and 6-\/bit mantissa for x component, a 5-\/bit biased exponent and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{388         \textcolor{comment}{// 6-\/bit mantissa for y component, a 5-\/bit biased exponent and a 5-\/bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{389         \textcolor{comment}{// mantissa for z. The z component is stored in the most significant bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{390         \textcolor{comment}{// and the x component in the least significant bits. No sign bits so}}
\DoxyCodeLine{391         \textcolor{comment}{// all partial-\/precision numbers are positive.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{392         \textcolor{comment}{// (Z10Y11X11): [32] ZZZZZzzz zzzYYYYY yyyyyyXX XXXxxxxx [0]}}

\DoxyCodeLine{427         \textcolor{comment}{// 3D vector: 9/9/9 floating-\/point components with shared 5-\/bit exponent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{428         \textcolor{comment}{// The 3D vector is packed into 32 bits as follows: a 5-\/bit biased exponent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{429         \textcolor{comment}{// with 9-\/bit mantissa for the x, y, and z component. The shared exponent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{430         \textcolor{comment}{// is stored in the most significant bits and the x component mantissa is in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{431         \textcolor{comment}{// the least significant bits. No sign bits so all partial-\/precision numbers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{432         \textcolor{comment}{// are positive.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{433         \textcolor{comment}{// (E5Z9Y9X9): [32] EEEEEzzz zzzzzzyy yyyyyyyx xxxxxxxx [0]}}
